             know all the words !!  ehe, well this music takes me
             back in time, when life was good! these days my life
             sucks, there  is nothing,  no meaning  or whatever!!
             well hopefully it goes  better way, when I go  study
             at  autumn (in Loimaa, after assembly96) krhm, so my
             board will be open, I'll move it to my parents place
             so the number should be the same!! keep calling heh!

             hm, this is my last  collection, atleas for a while!

             Ah,  just   watched  Prodigy's  Firestarter,  and  I
             fuckin'  love  it.  It gives me  so twisted feeling.
             I go  mad, when I listen  that song, It's  the best!
             Now I  would like to  go outside  and do some  crazy
             things  and  after  that people  thinks  I'm lunatic
             ehe, well it would't be the first time krhm, perhaps
             I am  a weird  person, who  knows! ( I know, I am!!)

             Hm, I made few  oldskool logos  for xCz, damn I love
             them, ehe!  especially the  first one, oldest style!
             wayback  in '93 uhm.. so I  hope ya mate are happy:)
             but It's damn  hard  to make  those logos,  ya  know
             after 3  years, must make  with the  same style etc.
             uaah, but I handle it quite good, krhm, or something
             like  that,  eh? why  do I write  all  this  text ?!

             I have a  real good feeling  now,  heh just  read my
             old  collys (late 1995),  heh I  have  been  writing
             allkinda  bullshit about my life etc. heh, damn it's
             funny  to read those now:) hm, well I hope I'll have
             vivid life  soon, eh cos I'm  going to  study  after
             assembly 1996!  just wondering  cos I had  so lively
             winter  b'cos I was  at  studying. I love  studying,
             especially   in a school-residence.  It's so  fun!:)
             Hm, oki  well I like  having fun, the studying ain't
             so fun heh but ya know what I mean !!  I hope so heh
